### [96] [Simulation of Axion-Induced Electromagnetic Signal Detection Using Plasmonic Metasurfaces and Diamond NV Centers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00068)
*James L. Webb*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于等离子体增强、异步检测和金刚石氮空位中心量子传感的实验室高灵敏度太赫兹频段轴子探测器，针对0.01–1 eV质量范围的轴子进行数值模拟与可行性分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有实验和天文观测已排除了大部分轴子质量-光子耦合参数空间，但在0.01–1 eV（对应THz频率）的高轴子质量区间仍缺乏高灵敏度探测手段。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法，结合纳米结构超表面的等离子体电场增强、异步检测技术以及金刚石中氮空位（NV）中心的量子传感，构建并评估轴子探测器性能；使用Ti/Au纳米柱/LiNbO₃结构在≈0.8 eV（196 THz）处建模，并探索CdTe等替代材料在更低质量（10⁻²–10⁻¹ eV）区间的适用性。

Result: 初步估计表明该传感器对轴子耦合产生的异常电磁场具有可观测响应；CdTe等材料有望拓展探测至更低轴子质量范围。

Conclusion: 所提出的基于纳米光子与固态量子传感融合的方案，在THz频段轴子探测中具备可行性，为填补高能轴子参数空间提供了新实验路径。

Abstract: The axion represents a strong candidate for weakly interacting dark matter. To date, high sensitivity lab based experiments and astrophysical observations have ruled out a substantial part of the axion mass and photon coupling parameter space. However, a challenge remains in searching for the presence of the axion in the higher mass range 0.01-1eV corresponding approximately to axion field oscillation at THz frequencies. This work investigates via numerical simulation the feasibility of a high sensitivity, lab-based axion sensor operating in this range, based on plasmonic electric field enhancement by a nanostructured metasurface, combined with heterodyne detection and quantum sensing via nitrogen-vacancy (NV) centers in diamond. Estimates of the sensor response to anomalous electromagnetic fields resulting from axion coupling are given using Ti/Au nanopillars on LiNb at axion mass corresponding to telecommunications wavelength ($\approx$0.8eV, 196 THz). Finally, the possibility of sensing in the lower axion mass $<$10$^{-2}$ to 10$^{-1}$eV range is explored using alternative materials, with CdTe as an example.

</details>


### [97] [Precision Solar System Dynamics for Ultralight Dark Matter Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00072)
*Jonas Frerick,Hyungjin Kim,Felix Kling*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文探讨了利用太阳系内高精度行星际无线电测距技术探测超轻暗物质的可能性，指出当前测量精度可在暗物质密度比局域暗物质密度高10^5倍时，探测到质量约为10^{-15} eV的超轻暗物质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超轻暗物质在波长尺度上具有量级为1的密度涨落，这种涨落遍布整个暗物质晕，并通过引力相互作用扰动恒星和行星运动；作者旨在探索是否可利用太阳系内高精度天体动力学观测来探测此类暗物质。

Method: 采用行星际无线电测距（interplanetary radio range measurements）数据分析方法，评估当前测距精度对超轻暗物质的探测能力。

Result: 当前测距精度可在暗物质局部密度增强10^5倍的假设下，探测质量约为10^{-15} eV的超轻暗物质；该结果补充了脉冲星计时等其他探测手段的限制。

Conclusion: 太阳系动力学是探测超轻暗物质的一个有潜力的新探针，尤其在特定质量与密度假设下可提供互补约束。

Abstract: Ultralight dark matter exhibits an order-one density fluctuation at the scale of its wavelength. This density fluctuation exists across the entire dark matter halo and interacts with stars and planets, perturbing their motion via gravitational interactions. We investigate the possibility of using precision solar system dynamics to search for ultralight dark matter. We examine this possibility with interplanetary radio range measurements. We show that the precision of current range measurements can probe ultralight dark matter at masses around $10^{-15}\,$eV, had its density in the solar system been $10^5$ larger than the so-called local dark matter density. This limit complements other constraints, such as the one from analyses of pulsar timing observations.

</details>


### [98] [Putting Jet Substructure on Track(s)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00087)
*Kyle Lee,Ian Moult,Wouter J. Waalewijn*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次在LHC上基于带电粒子径迹完整计算了喷注子结构可观测量，达到次领头对数精度，提升了理论与实验对比的精度和系统可改进性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为提升喷注子结构测量的精度并研究更细微的关联性，需利用径迹信息实现卓越的角度分辨率。

Method: 基于因子化定理和重整化群技术的最新进展，计算了直至四点投影能量关联器（track-based）在次领头对数精度下的结果。

Result: 首次实现了LHC上基于径迹的喷注子结构可观测量的完整理论计算，达到当前喷注子结构研究的最高精度水平。

Conclusion: 该工作显著推动了对撞机物理研究，使基于高角分辨率径迹的精确、系统可改进的理论-实验比对成为可能。

Abstract: One of the main advances in analysis strategies at the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) has been the ability to study the detailed structure of energy flow within high transverse momentum jets, a field referred to as jet substructure. Jet substructure has provided new ways to search for new physics, measure Standard Model parameters, and study the dynamics of the strong nuclear force. To push to the next level of precision, and to make measurements of increasingly subtle correlations, requires exquisite angular resolution achieved through the use of tracking information. In this paper we leverage recent progress in our understanding of factorization theorems and renormalization group techniques to present the first complete calculations of jet substructure observables at the LHC on tracks. We compute projected energy correlators up to four points at next-to-leading collinear logarithmic accuracy, matching the state of the art for jet substructure observables, but extending to tracks. This marks a significant step in enhancing the collider physics program, enabling precise and systematically improvable comparisons between experimental measurements and theoretical calculations, made possible by the exceptional angular resolution of tracking.

</details>


### [99] [The left-cut for partial waves in terms of physical amplitudes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00136)
*Alexandre Salas-Bernárdez*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文推导出2→2散射中左支割线部分波振幅的新表示，将任意同位旋和角动量的部分波左支割线表达为右支割线虚部的积分，从而显式、精确地提取对数型支割线结构，为逆振幅法或N/D等幺正化方法中的左支割线不确定性提供了系统量化工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为系统量化幺正化方法（如逆振幅法或N/D方法）中左支割线带来的不确定性，需明确其数学结构与来源。

Method: 推导2→2散射中任意同位旋和角动量部分波的左支割线振幅新表示，将其表达为右支割线虚部的积分形式。

Result: 获得左支割线的显式、精确积分表达式，成功提取其对数型分支割线结构。

Conclusion: 该新表示为幺正化方法中左支割线效应的定量分析提供了严格且实用的理论工具。

Abstract: We derive a novel representation of the partial wave amplitude over the left-hand cut for $2 \to 2$ scattering. We express the left-hand cut of arbitrary isospin and angular momentum partial waves as an integral of right-hand cut imaginary parts. This formulation provides an explicit, exact extraction of the logarithmic branch cut structures, offering a valuable tool to systematically quantify left-hand cut uncertainties in unitarization methods such as the Inverse Amplitude Method or $N/D$ approaches.

</details>


### [100] [Production of Magic States via $Z$ Bosons and Dark Photons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00229)
*Carlos Alvarado,Alfredo Aranda,César Bonilla,Yahir Lua,Ethan Rodríguez-Martínez*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了标准模型电弱部门及含新破缺U(1)规范对称性的扩展模型中魔态（magic states）的产生，分析了不同能量区域下的魔态分布函数与稳定子态分类变化，并识别出在不同能区下保持不变的固定稳定子态子集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 魔态是量子计算中实现通用量子门的关键资源，其产生机制在粒子物理过程中尚未被系统研究；本文旨在探索标准模型及其暗物质扩展中魔态产生的新机制与特征。

Method: 基于量子场论框架，分别分析标准模型电弱相互作用（包括低能、高能及Z共振区）以及含新U(1)规范玻色子和带电暗费米子的扩展模型中的散射过程（如Bhabha、Møller类及逆湮灭过程），计算并比较各过程的魔态分布函数与稳定子态结构。

Result: 在电弱部门中，低能区复现QED已有结果，高能与Z共振区产生新魔态分布并重构稳定子态分类，Bhabha散射对电弱效应最敏感；发现一组魔态分布不随能区变化的固定稳定子态；在暗部门中，新规范玻色子导致低能下出现新的魔态分布，在mf/mχ→0和mf/mχ→1.83929时达到最大魔值。

Conclusion: 魔态产生具有丰富的粒子物理依赖性，电弱效应与新暗规范相互作用均可显著调控魔态分布与稳定子结构，为量子信息与高能物理交叉研究提供新视角与潜在探针。

Abstract: The production of magic states is studied in two settings. The first is the electroweak (EW) sector of the Standard Model (SM). The second is an extension featuring a new broken $U(1)$ gauge symmetry and a Dirac fermion charged under it. This setup resembles a dark $U(1)$ scenario, with the additional fermion playing the role of a dark matter candidate that annihilates into SM particles through its coupling to the new gauge boson. In the EW sector, the low-energy regime reproduces earlier magic production results obtained for Quantum Electrodynamics, whereas the high-energy and $Z$-resonance regimes generate new magic distribution functions and non-trivially reorganize the stabilizer state classes, with Bhabha scattering exhibiting the strongest sensitivity to electroweak effects. Also, a subset of fixed stabilizer states is identified, for which the magic distributions remain unchanged across the different energy regimes. In the dark sector, the main effect of the new massive mediator is the appearance of new magic distributions functions for Moller-like, Bhabha-like, and inverse pair-annihilation processes in the low-energy limit. These reach the maximal magic value at the SM-to-dark fermion mass ratios $m_f/m_χ\to 0$ and $m_f/m_χ\to 1.83929$.

</details>


### [101] [Soft-Dimuon Signature from Two-Component Scalar Dark Matter at the LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00243)
*Alexander Belyaev,Manimala Chakraborti,Shu Chen,Atri Dey,Venus Keus,Rakhi Mahbubani,Stefano Moretti*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了大型强子对撞机（LHC）在双组分标量暗物质模型中通过同号/反号μ子对加缺失横向能量加硬喷注末态探测暗物质的能力，基于一个含一个活跃和两个惰性希格斯二重态的三希格斯二重态模型（3HDM），利用Z₂×Z₂′对称性稳定两个惰性扇区中最轻中性标量，形成两个暗物质候选者；通过蒙特卡洛模拟与定制化切口分析，在LHC Run 3及未来高亮度升级下评估信号显著性，并指出虽然事例中存在双峰结构，但经优化切口后该特征不足以确认双组分起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索LHC在反号双μ子+缺失横动量+硬喷注末态中探测双组分标量暗物质的可能性，弥补宇宙学观测与对撞机探测之间的互补空白，并检验多组分暗物质模型的可证伪性。

Method: 构建具有Z₂×Z₂′对称性的三希格斯二重态模型（I(2+1)HDM），其中两个惰性扇区各自提供一个稳定暗物质候选者；开展探测器层次的蒙特卡洛模拟，设计针对软双μ系统（m_μμ ≪ m_Z）与级联衰变拓扑的专用切口策略，包括适配信号的横质量（m_T）要求。

Result: 在Run 3（300 fb⁻¹）下获得信噪比S/B≈9.8%，统计显著性S/√B=1.35；外推至4 ab⁻¹时达S/√B=4.93；事例初态呈现双峰型μμ不变质量分布，但经优化切口后该结构统计不显著，无法确证双组分起源；所选基准点为亚主导（subdominant）双组分暗物质场景。

Conclusion: LHC可在特定参数空间下灵敏探测双组分标量暗物质，尤其适用于弱相互作用、电弱关联产生且存在小于m_Z质量分裂的级联衰变场景；尽管当前显著性尚不足以发现，但高亮度LHC阶段有望达到可观测水平；结果具有一般性，可推广至类似拓扑的多暗物质模型。

Abstract: We explore the potential of the Large Hadron Collider to probe a two-component scalar dark matter scenario in the opposite-sign dimuon plus missing transverse energy final state, accompanied by a hard jet. The signal features a soft dimuon system with an invariant mass well below $m_Z$. We consider a 3-Higgs Doublet Model with one active and two inert scalar doublets, where a $Z_2 \times Z_2'$ symmetry stabilises the lightest neutral scalar in each inert sector, yielding two scalar DM candidates. The relevant parameter space is mapped in terms of the two DM masses and the mass splittings between each DM candidate and its corresponding next-to-lightest scalar state. We perform a detector-level Monte Carlo analysis and design a dedicated cut-based selection, including a transverse-mass requirement adapted to the signal topology. For a representative benchmark, we obtain $S/B\simeq 9.8%$ and a statistical-only significance of $S/\sqrt{B}=1.35$ at Run 3 with ${\cal L}=300~{\rm fb}^{-1}$, increasing to $S/\sqrt{B}=4.93$ under a statistical-only extrapolation to ${\cal L}=4~{\rm ab}^{-1}$. Before the full selection, the two dark sectors generate a double-bump structure in the dimuon invariant-mass distribution. After the cuts optimised for inclusive sensitivity, however, this feature is not statistically robust enough to establish the two-component origin of the signal. The benchmark is underabundant and is interpreted as a subdominant two-component DM scenario, while the collider analysis remains independent of its cosmological abundance. Although the numerical study is carried out in the I(2+1)HDM, the results are applicable to weakly interacting sectors with similar electroweak associated production and cascade decays, where a heavier state separated from the DM candidate by less than $m_Z$ produces a soft muon pair via an off-shell $Z$ boson.

</details>


### [102] [Classifying the hidden-charm pentaquarks via a flavor mixing scheme](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00411)
*Kan Chen,Bo Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于轻味自由度分类的重子-介子分子态框架，用于系统解释已观测到的Pc和Pcs态，并预测单奇异和双奇异隐粲束缚态的存在及质量谱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为统一解释实验上发现的Pc和Pcs类奇特强子态，并预测尚未观测到的奇异隐粲分子态。

Method: 基于轻味自由度对含单粲重子与反D(*)/Ds(*)介子构成的分子态进行分类；利用通道混合机制（如Σc(*)Ds(*)与Ξ′c(*)D(*)混合）分析吸引力来源；通过拟合已知Pc/Pcs参数预测新态质量谱。

Result: 成功一致解释Pc和Pcs态；预测存在单奇异和双奇异隐粲束缚态；给出其系统性质量谱。

Conclusion: 该分类框架不仅合理解释已有实验现象，还为寻找新型奇异隐粲分子态提供了明确理论指引和可检验预言。

Abstract: In this work, we propose a scheme to classify the molecular states consisting of ground single-charm baryons ($Λ_c$, $Ξ_c$, $Σ_c^{(*)}$, $Ξ_c^{\prime(*)}$, $Ω_c^{(*)}$) and $\bar{D}^{(*)}/\bar{D}_s^{(*)}$ mesons. Within this framework, all considered baryon-meson systems are categorized according to the flavor components of their light degrees of freedom. We briefly illustrate how this classification scheme can consistently explain the experimentally observed $P_c$ and $P_{cs}$ states. This framework also predicts the existences of single-strange and double-strange hidden-charm bound states. The attractive interactions of these states arise from channel mixing between $Σ_c^{(*)}\bar{D}_s^{(*)}$ and $Ξ_c^{\prime(*)}\bar{D}^{(*)}$ for single-strange systems, and mixing between $Ξ_c^{\prime(*)}\bar{D}_s^{(*)}$ and $Ω_c^{(*)}\bar{D}^{(*)}$ for double-strange systems, respectively. Using parameters fitted from the measured $P_c$ and $P_{cs}$ states, we systematically present the predicted mass spectra for these single- and double-strange hidden-charm bound states.

</details>


### [103] [Fermion Mixing Matrices and the Exceptional Jordan Algebra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00412)
*Bishnu Gupta Teli,Tejinder P. Singh*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文将例外约旦谱框架扩展到夸克和轻子混合问题，利用八元数阶梯算符和Fritzsch型纹理构建了从质量谱到混合角的映射，提出了一个描述卡比博相位关系的有效桥接假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将已有的例外约旦谱框架（用于费米子质量等级）推广至解释夸克与轻子混合角的起源，特别是CKM和PMNS矩阵中的相位结构。

Method: 基于J₃(𝕆_ℂ)上的厄米特元素构建费米子扇区模型，通过立方阶梯获得相邻质量比，并以此输入构建两代混合角的‘邻边提升’；引入Fritzsch型两态纹理作为有效桥接假设，并结合CP输运输入（来自配套论文）。

Result: 推导出卡比博层级相位律φ₁₂ = −2χ，在拟合质量比后得到有效卡比博块相位φ₁₂ ≈ 105.7°；(2,3)扇区需经验归一化κ₂₃ ≈ 0.56，(1,3)元素仍为待解长边桥接问题。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一种基于八元数代数和约旦谱的新型混合角生成机制，但当前结果依赖于有效桥接假设和经验参数，尚未构成严格谱定理推论。

Abstract: We extend the exceptional-Jordan spectral framework for fermion mass hierarchies to the problem of quark and lepton mixing. Following the companion mass paper~\cite{Teli:2026jgr}, each fermion sector is associated with a Hermitian element of $J_3(\mathbb{O}_{\mathbb{C}})$, where adjacent square-root mass ratios are obtained from cubic ladders in $\mathrm{Sym}^3(\mathbf 3)$. Here, these ratios are used as inputs to an adjacent-edge lift from spectral hierarchy data to two-generation mixing angles. The lift is derived from a Fritzsch-type two-state texture~\cite{Fritzsch:1977za, Fritzsch:1979zq} and should be regarded as an effective bridge ansatz rather than a theorem of the Jordan spectrum alone. The exact CP-transport input is supplied by the companion CP Letter~\cite{GuptaTeli:2026aqf}. In the quark sector, the octonionic ladder operator $α_2$ generates a real local rotor in the $(e_1,e_3)$ plane, and the up- and down-sector local Cabibbo-edge amplitudes are complex conjugates, giving the exact local law $φ_{12}=-2χ$. This is a transport-level Cabibbo-rung phase law, not by itself a prediction of the standard CKM Dirac phase. With the fitted companion mass ratios, the minimal two-angle extraction from the measured $|V_{us}|$ gives an effective Cabibbo-block phase $φ_{12}\simeq 105.7^\circ$; this number is a bridge diagnostic, while the balanced octonionic rotor remains the distinguished quadrature reference point. The $(2,3)$ sector requires a phenomenological normalization $κ_{23}\simeq0.56$, and the direct $(1,3)$ element remains a long-edge bridge problem. [Truncated]

</details>


### [104] [Sub-eikonal stress and model dependence of the small-$x$ gluon D-term](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00439)
*Lei Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文探讨了小-x区域中胶子D项的确定问题，指出传统的偶极子模型不足以确定胶子应力形式因子C_g(t)和D项，因为其依赖于次领头阶（next-to-eikonal）场和应力修饰的威尔逊线；作者构建了相应算符，并通过有限关联响应模型展示了负的前向D项，并指出D项本质上是次领头阶应力探针，而非饱和效应的普适可观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 胶子D项与胶子应力形式因子C_g(t)密切相关，但现有基于领头阶偶极子模型的方法无法唯一确定它，需厘清其是否为饱和效应的普适可观测量。

Method: 通过分析Drell-Yan参考系下能量动量张量分量的投影特性，构建包含次领头阶场F^{i-}、F^{ij}的规范不变应力修饰威尔逊线算符，并在树图水平匹配局域能量动量张量；进而提出有限关联响应模型，结合多种核型轮廓（高斯、Woods-Saxon等）进行数值扫描。

Result: 证明普通偶极子S_x(b_⊥,r_⊥)或饱和尺度Q_s^2(x,b)本身不能决定小-x胶子D项的符号；在反向对齐响应模型中，得到稳定的负前向D项D_g(0)<0及符合预期的核心-壳层压强分布。

Conclusion: 胶子D项是次领头阶应力探针，而非领头阶饱和可观测量；其符号与具体次领头阶动力学响应相关，不能仅由饱和模型推断。

Abstract: The leading-eikonal small-$x$ dipole gives a compact representation of the gluon momentum form factor $A_g(t)$. We show that the same information is not sufficient to determine the gluon stress form factor $C_g(t)$, and hence the gluon D-term. The reason is kinematic and operatorial: in a Drell-Yan frame $A_g(t)$ is projected by $T_g^{++}$, whereas $C_g(t)$ is projected by the symmetric-traceless transverse stress $T_g^{ij}$. This stress projection first appears through next-to-eikonal fields and is represented by gauge-invariant stress-decorated Wilson lines containing $F^{i-}$, $F^{ij}$, or equivalent sub-eikonal target fields. We construct this operator and match it to the local energy-momentum tensor at tree level, obtaining an operator-level no-go statement: the ordinary dipole $S_x(b_\perp,r_\perp)$, or a saturation profile $Q_s^2(x,b)$, does not by itself determine the sign of the small-$x$ gluon D-term. We then give a finite-correlation response model in which a positive kernel generates an anti-aligned response $F^{i-}=-εR_{\rm NE}F^{i+}$, so that $Λ_{\rm NE}>0$ and $D_g(0)<0$ within that response class. A Gaussian benchmark and numerical scans over Gaussian, Woods-Saxon, power-edge, and McLerran-Venugopalan (MV)-inspired profiles show a stable negative forward D-term for this anti-aligned model, together with the expected core-shell pressure pattern. The gluon D-term is therefore a next-to-eikonal stress probe, not a universal leading-eikonal saturation observable.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We investigate the multidimensional partonic structure of spin-0 mesons, specifically the pion and the kaon, by evaluating their complete set of eight generalized parton distributions (GPDs) up to twist-4. Utilizing the light-front quark model (LFQM) with the Brodsky-Huang-Lepage (BHL) prescription, we compute these distributions in the kinematically rich non-zero skewness ($ξ\neq 0$) domain, strictly within the DGLAP region, $x \in [ξ, 1]$. To construct a three-dimensional tomographic picture, we perform Fourier transforms of the momentum-space GPDs to obtain the impact parameter dependent parton distribution functions (IPDPDFs) in the transverse plane and the corresponding diffraction patterns in the longitudinal coordinate space. The numerical results explicitly reveal the consequences of $\mathrm{SU}(3)$ flavor symmetry breaking, as the strange quark in the kaon dynamically shifts spatial localizations compared to the lighter up quarks. TL;DR: 本文探讨了Δ(1232)粒子的πN部分衰变宽度异常大于其总宽度的现象，指出这是S矩阵幺正混合的自然结果，并通过一个启发式弹性模型揭示了复数极点处S矩阵微扰导致残差幅度系统性放大，从而表明复数残差反映的是整体散射振幅拓扑结构而非孤立本征性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释Δ(1232)粒子的πN部分衰变宽度（2|r|）系统性超过其总宽度Γ这一反常现象。

Method: 采用启发式弹性模型（将重叠的Δ(1600)视为完全弹性），结合S矩阵幺正性与复极点处的微扰分析，研究多通道阴影极点的影响。

Result: 证明在共振态复极点处评估微扰S矩阵会系统性放大残差模长；复数残差本质上反映全局散射振幅拓扑，而非局域本征属性。

Conclusion: 该异常是S矩阵幺正混合的自然体现；对分支比的朴素解读（如将|residue|²直接等同于物理分支比）存在根本性缺陷。

Abstract: The extracted $πN$ partial decay width of the $Δ(1232)$ systematically exceeds its total width ($2|r|>Γ$). We demonstrate this anomaly is a natural consequence of S-matrix unitary mixing. Because exact multi-channel shadow poles are distant and model-dependent, we utilize a heuristic elastic model -- treating the overlapping $Δ(1600)$ as fully elastic -- to isolate the core mechanism. We show that evaluating a perturbing S-matrix at a state's complex pole systematically inflates the residue magnitude. This proof of principle confirms complex residues reflect global amplitude topology rather than isolated intrinsic properties, challenging naive interpretations of branching fractions.

</details>


### [115] [Exploring the neutron momentum distribution in nuclei through $γn \to π^- p$ at an electron-positron collider](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00783)
*Zi-Wei Yan,Shu-man Hu,Wei Wang,Ji Xu,Fu-Sheng Yu,Ya-Teng Zhang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出利用北京谱仪III（BESIII）的铍束流管研究γn→π⁻p过程，以精确测量中子动量分布，进而提取自由中子基本观测量并探究短程关联和张量力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中子动量分布对从核实验中可靠提取自由中子基本观测量、以及通过高动量中子组分研究张量力与短程关联（SRCs）至关重要。

Method: 在冲量近似框架下计算氘核和铍靶上γn→π⁻p过程的截面，并结合BESIII实验装置中靶材料分布，评估来自辐射Bhabha散射的光子通量有效亮度。

Result: 结果表明BESIII可产生数万个事例，有望实现中子动量分布的精确测量。

Conclusion: 电子-正电子对撞机可在核结构研究和非微扰QCD理解中发挥重要作用，为粒子物理与核物理提供新研究途径。

Abstract: The neutron momentum distribution is essential both for reliably extracting fundamental free neutron observables from nuclear measurements and for probing the tensor force via the high-momentum neutron fraction, which is crucial to the theoretical understanding of short-range correlations (SRCs). In this work, we investigate this distribution by studying the $γn \to π^- p$ process at an electron-positron collider, proposing to utilize the beryllium beam pipe at the Beijing Spectrometer III (BESIII). The cross sections for this process on both deuteron and beryllium targets are calculated within the impulse approximation framework. We also evaluate the effective luminosity of the photon flux from radiative Bhabha scattering, taking into account the distribution of target materials within the BESIII experimental setup. Our results show that tens of thousands of events can be generated at BESIII, offering the potential for precise measurements of the neutron momentum distribution. These findings suggest that electron-positron colliders could play a valuable role in elucidating nuclear structure and advancing our understanding of nonperturbative QCD, offering promising new avenues for both particle and nuclear physics.

### [116] [Dark matter energy exchange in stars orbiting supermassive black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00840)
*Stephan A. Meighen-Berger,R. Andrew Gustafson,Nicole F. Bell,Jayden L. Newstead,Sandra Robles,Ian M. Shoemaker*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 计算S4714恒星在尖峰型暗物质密度分布下的轨道平均暗物质诱导能量交换，并结合不同质量区间（MeV–GeV与亚MeV）的暗物质-核子/电子散射截面进行分析。

Result: 对于MeV–GeV质量暗物质，σ_χp ~ 10⁻³⁶ cm²；对亚MeV质量暗物质，σ_χe ~ 5×10⁻³⁸ cm²时，能量交换可达恒星光度量级，可触发暗星相；这些截面值与冻入机制预言及宇宙线增强、太阳反射等实验约束一致。

Conclusion: 暗物质与紧密轨道恒星的能量交换提供了一种新的、无需湮灭的暗星形成机制，且相关参数处于当前理论与观测可容许范围内，为探测非湮灭型暗物质开辟新途径。

Abstract: Stars on tight orbits around the supermassive black hole at the Galactic Center pass through regions where the dark matter~(DM) density may be strongly enhanced. We compute the orbit-averaged DM-induced energy exchange for S4714 as an example. It is a star on an exceptionally close and relativistic orbit around Sagittarius~A*. For a spiked dark matter profile, the exchange reaches the stellar luminosity at $σ_{χp} \sim 10^{-36}~\mathrm{cm}^2$ for MeV-GeV masses and $σ_{χe} \sim 5\times10^{-38}~\mathrm{cm}^2$ for sub-MeV masses, opening a new annihilation-free route toward dark-star phases. These cross sections lie within the range predicted by freeze-in scenarios and are consistent with cosmic-ray--boosted and solar-reflection dark matter constraints.

### [118] [Quantum entanglement of photon pairs at proton-proton colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.00971)
*Yue Pan,Yipin Wang,Leyun Gao,Qiang Li,Chen Zhou*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在质子-质子对撞机上测量双光子系统量子纠缠的新方法，利用追踪器中的Bethe-Heitler过程分析光子自旋，通过电子-正电子对的联合角分布提取偏振信息；模拟显示，在HL-LHC条件下，Higgs→γγ过程的纠缠显著性仅为0.007σ，而连续谱qq̄→γγ过程可达约1.5σ。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用追踪器中光子与原子核发生Bethe-Heitler过程产生e⁺e⁻对，其联合角分布携带双光子偏振信息，从而实现对纠缠的间接测量。

Result: 在HL-LHC条件下，Higgs→γγ过程的纠缠统计显著性为0.007σ，而连续谱qq̄→γγ过程可达约1.5σ。

Conclusion: 该方法为高能对撞机上探测双光子纠缠提供了可行路径，尽管Higgs衰变信号极弱，但强本底过程（如qq̄→γγ）已具备初步可观测性，为未来高精度量子测量开辟新方向。

Abstract: Diphoton systems, with photon polarizations measurable at low energies, serve as ideal qubits and were first used to demonstrate quantum entanglement. However, due to the current absence of dedicated polarimeters at high-energy colliders, the entanglement properties of diphoton systems remain largely unexplored at the high-energy frontier. Studying quantum entanglement at the high-energy frontier, where particle colliders serve as a natural relativistic laboratory, helps us better understand the quantum nature and seek new physics. In this letter, we propose a novel method to measure the entanglement of diphoton systems at proton-proton colliders. The photon spin analyzing power arises from the Bethe-Heitler process occurring in the tracker, where photons scatter off nuclei to produce electron-positron pairs whose joint angular distribution encodes the polarization of the diphoton system. Simulation results show that, under HL-LHC conditions, the statistical significance of quantum entanglement in the Higgs $\to γγ$ process is $0.007σ$, while measuring the continuum diphoton process $q\bar{q} \to γγ$ alone can reach about $1.5σ$.

### [120] [Shedding light on the nature of $φ(2170)$ with the parton and hadron cascade model PACIAE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01075)
*Jian Cao,Wen-Chao Zhang,Bo Feng,Ya-Hui Hou,An-Ke Lei,Zhi-Lei She,Hua Zheng,Li-Lin Zhu,Dai-Mei Zhou,Yu-Liang Yan,Ben-Hao Sa*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过PACIAE 4.0模拟e⁺e⁻对撞中φ(2170)的产生，系统评估其多种可能的内部结构（如激发态奇异偶素、混合态、四夸克态、Λ̄Λ束缚态、φK⁺K⁻共振态等），基于轨道角动量分类与产额、快度分布和横动量谱的差异，为鉴别其真实结构提供关键判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: φ(2170)的内部结构尚未确定，现有解释包括ss̄s̄s、uūs̄s等四夸克态，但U(1)反常耦合提示非奇异夸克可通过软胶子与s̄s耦合，因此需拓展考虑dđs̄s等新构型，并系统比较多种候选结构。

Method: 采用PACIAE 4.0模型在√s=4.95 GeV下模拟e⁺e⁻碰撞，依次生成末态部分子态（FPS）和末态强子态（FHS）；对奇异偶素、混合态、四夸克态采用动力学约束相空间并合模型在FPS中形成；对Λ̄Λ和φK⁺K⁻则在FHS中通过强子重组生成；计算各候选态静止系中的轨道角动量并进行谱学分类。

Result: 在J^(PC)=1^(−−)约束下，φ(2170)可对应D波s̄s、P波s̄sg、P波uūs̄s/dđs̄s/ss̄s̄s、S波Λ̄Λ或S波φK⁺K⁻态；产额分别为~10⁻⁴、~10⁻⁴、~10⁻⁴/~10⁻⁴/~10⁻⁶、~10⁻⁵、~10⁻⁵；各候选态在快度分布和p_T谱上存在显著差异。

Conclusion: φ(2170)的多种结构假说均在理论上可行，但其产额大小及动力学分布（快度、p_T）存在明显区分，这些可观测差异可作为未来实验甄别其真实结构的关键判据。

Abstract: The nature of $φ(2170)$ remains open. We simulate its production in $e^+e^-$ collisions at $\sqrt{s}=4.95$ GeV using PACIAE 4.0, which sequentially generates the final partonic state (FPS) and the final hadronic state (FHS). While previous studies have interpreted $φ(2170)$ as an $ss\bar{s}\bar{s}$ or $u\bar{u}s\bar{s}$ state, the $U(1)$ anomaly coupling allows non-strange quarks to couple to a vector $s\bar{s}$ component via soft-gluon interactions. This motivates us to also explore the $d\bar{d}s\bar{s}$ tetraquark configuration. In addition, we consider $φ(2170)$ as an excited strangeonium state, an $s\bar{s}g$ hybrid state, a $\barΛΛ$ bound state, and a $φK^+K^-$ resonance state. The strangeonium, hybrid, and tetraquark candidates are formed by coalescing their constituent partons in the FPS using the dynamically constrained phase-space coalescence model. The $\barΛΛ$ and $φK^+K^-$ states are produced via recombination of their constituent hadrons in the FHS. We calculate the orbital angular momentum quantum number of each candidate in its rest frame and perform spectral classification. Given $J^{PC}=1^{--}$, $φ(2170)$ can be interpreted as a $D$-wave $s\bar{s}$, a $P$-wave $s\bar{s}g$, a $P$-wave $u\bar{u}s\bar{s}/d\bar{d}s\bar{s}/ss\bar{s}\bar{s}$, an $S$-wave $\barΛΛ$, or an $S$-wave $φK^+K^-$ state. The yields of the $D$-wave $s\bar{s}$, $P$-wave $s\bar{s}g$, $u\bar{u}s\bar{s}$ and $d\bar{d}s\bar{s}$ states are of order $10^{-4}$; those for the $S$-wave $\barΛΛ$ and $φK^+K^-$ states are of order $10^{-5}$; while the $P$-wave $ss\bar{s}\bar{s}$ yield is of order $10^{-6}$. Moreover, significant discrepancies are observed in the rapidity distributions and the $p_T$ spectra among the various candidates. These discrepancies could serve as valuable criteria for unraveling the nature of $φ(2170)$.

</details>


### [121] [HyperFORM -- a FORM package for parametric integration with hyperlogarithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01163)
*Adam Kardos,Sven-Olaf Moch,Oliver Schnetz*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: HyperFORM is a new package that integrates hyperlogarithms with rational prefactors in the symbolic-manipulation system FORM, leveraging its speed and parallel computing capabilities. It is inspired by HyperInt and targets Feynman integral evaluations.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To bring efficient, parallelizable parametric integration of hyperlogarithms—weighted by rational prefactors—into FORM, enabling high-performance evaluation of complex integrals like Feynman integrals.

Method: Ports HyperInt’s algorithmic capabilities into FORM; uses FORM’s optimized algebraic processing and multi-core distribution; includes a self-contained three-loop zigzag period example and scalability tests up to six loops.

Result: A fully functional, open-source HyperFORM package capable of evaluating zigzag periods up to six loops; demonstrates strong performance and broad applicability to Feynman integrals.

Conclusion: HyperFORM successfully extends FORM’s capabilities for hyperlogarithmic integration, offering speed, scalability, and openness for applications in quantum field theory and related domains.

Abstract: HyperFORM brings the parametric integration of hyperlogarithms, weighted by rational prefactors, into the symbolic-manipulation system FORM. It ports the capabilities of Erik Panzer's Maple package HyperInt, capitalizing on FORM's speed with bulky algebraic input and on its ability to spread a single calculation across many processor cores. We keep the description of the method brief and concentrate instead on how the package is organized and driven: a fully self-contained program for the three-loop zigzag period serves as a worked illustration, and timing measurements for zigzags through six loops gauge its present reach. HyperFORM is released openly and applies to a broad class of problems, the evaluation of Feynman integrals prominently among them.

### [122] [The cleanest of them all: NLO electroweak corrections to vector-boson scattering into doubly polarised ZZ pairs at the LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01174)
*Ansgar Denner,Robert Franken,Santiago Lopez Portillo Chavez,Daniele Lombardi,Giovanni Pelliccioli*

TL;DR: 本文首次计算了LHC上双极化Z玻色子矢量玻色子散射过程的下一阶电弱修正，采用双极点近似一致建模Z玻色子产生与衰变，并在振幅层面分离极化态，包含可因子化的实虚电弱修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为提升矢量玻色子散射过程理论预测精度，支持LHC Run-3及高亮度升级的数据分析，并推动相关唯象学研究。

Method: 采用双极点近似建模双极化Z玻色子的产生与衰变，在振幅层面分离极化态，并纳入可因子化的实和虚电弱辐射修正。

Result: 给出了积分与微分层次下双极化及非极化信号的结果，并与离壳结果进行了对比；所有分析基于CMS启发式的现实层析（fiducial）设置。

Conclusion: 该工作为LHC Run-3和高亮度LHC数据的后续分析奠定理论基础，并拓展了对电弱精确测量的唯象研究路径。

Abstract: We present the first calculation of the next-to-leading-order electroweak corrections to vector-boson scattering into doubly polarised Z bosons at the LHC in the fully leptonic decay channel. The production and decay of the two polarised Z bosons are consistently modelled in the double-pole approximation, separating polarisation states at the amplitude level and including factorisable real and virtual electroweak corrections. Doubly polarised and unpolarised signals are investigated and confronted with off-shell results. A broad analysis, including results at integrated and differential level, is carried out in a realistic, CMS-inspired fiducial setup. Our study paves the way to upcoming analyses with LHC Run-3 and High-Luminosity data as well as to further phenomenological investigations.
